 0pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 10
 0pt; font-family:"calibri","sans-serif"; mso-ascii-font-family:calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin; mso-hansi-font-family:calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;}< / style><![endif](iccceyaramenapaxa se shashaank manohar kaa istipha,abhi 16maah kaa bachaa tha kaarykaal)isisi ke vaarshik sammelan tak pad par bane rahane ko taiyaarunhone kaha, ‘meri jimmedaari he ki apane saathiyon ke saath sabhi prakriyaayein acchhee tarah puri ho, iskaa dhyaan rakhun
 Cricket Australia Chairman David Peaver said, "it is clear from the proposal that even though some members may not agree with the action of our reform, we all trust Shashank and we want the whole process to be done with him
" hamen khushi he ki wo 2017 ke vaarshik sammelan tak pad par bane rahane ke liye raji ho gaye hai
 bcci's Vikram Limaye said, "it is important that the solution to the recent issues is to satisfy everyone
" hamaari haal main manohar ke saath meeting (istipha dene se pehle) hui thi
 We briefed him about the bcci's concern on financial and governance issues
 hamane apni taraf se salaah bhi di thi
 We are ready to work with the ICC to resolve these issues
 ’ Regarding the crushing defeat of Congress in Uttar Pradesh and Uttarakhand election results, former party MP Sandeep Dixit said that Congress needs leaders, not clerks
 sandip dikshit ne iske saath hi party netritv ko lekar shikayati lahaze main kaha ki haar kii jimmedaari rahul kii bhi banati he
 The Congress has become a joke in UP
 upi main kabhi congress kii siem ummidavaar banaai gayi shila dikshit ke bete sandip kehete hai, 'congress apni chunavi nitiyon ko lekar kanphyus he
 The Congress had moved ahead with a strong strategy after 15-20 years in UP, we should have walked the same way
 ' vah kehete hai, 'ham ye jaanate the ki sarkaar nahin banane vaali, lekin phir bhi 30-40 siten to jeet hi lete or isse aage bhi ja sakate hai
 'see the complete list of victorious candidates for the UP elections,' but Rahul ji's journey suddenly broke
 kyon hua
 
 
 What happened
 
 
 main nahin jaanata
 He says that even if there was to be an alliance with the SP, before that there was no justification for applying the brakes after the journey from Delhi to Deoria
 isse hamane baari nuksaan kar liya
 Questioning the Congress leadership and its strategy, Sandeep says, "the Congress party has become a joke
 ' vahiin upi main haar kii zimmedaari ke sawaal par vah kehete hai, 'yah sabaki jimmedaari banati he
 No one can be left out, even if it is Rachel Gandhi
 
 
 unki bhi zimmedaari he
 Advising the Congress to return to its original policies, Sandeep says, "after every defeat, there is talk of introspection, but the truth is that till date there has been no analysis
" jab tak aap maanenge nahin ki aapane galat kiyaai or nae sire se ranneeti banaaenge, tab tak vishleshan kaa bhi kya phayda
 You may be wrong, or you may not know what to do next
 to charchaa kariye
 But what will happen when only those responsible for the defeat are analyzed
 haalanki iske baavjood sandip dikshit kii ummiden jinda hai
 He says that after the victories in Punjab and Goa, it is certain that the Congress is the biggest opposition party
 ye mauka bhi he ki ham congress kii puraani nitiyon par lauten
 Do a true self-belief
 nae logon ko mauka den, vahiin hamen satta main waapas pahunchaayenge
 Amid mounting attacks on Telecom Minister a Raja in the backdrop of the alleged scam in spectrum allocation, the Congress left the decision on Raja's future to the DMK
